Telegram Request from the Overseas Chinese Federation

Amendment to the Chamber of Commerce Law 120

Detailed Rules, Article 41

The Overseas Chinese Federation sent a telegram to the assembly, stating: "To the Chairman and Vice-Chairmen and all members of the National Industrial and Commercial Conference in Nanjing: We have repeatedly received telegrams and letters from the Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce requesting that you appeal for the amendment of Article 41 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Chamber of Commerce Law (Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce will be renamed Overseas Chinese Chambers of Commerce under this law) during your conference, so that the Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce can continue to use their old names. The reason is that the Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce use the Malay transliteration (TiongHwaTjongSiangHwee) as their name, which has been approved for registration by the residing government. All contracts and properties are handled under the aforementioned (Malay transliteration name). Once the name is changed to Overseas Chinese Chambers of Commerce, it will not only seem different to us, but also appear completely different to the residing government. It will be necessary to revise the foreign articles of association and re-apply to the residing government for examination and registration. The residing government has long witnessed that various Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce are wholeheartedly supporting the motherland and assisting the revolution, which is like a thorn in their side. They have repeatedly considered suppressing them, but because each General Chamber of Commerce has been approved for registration for decades, it is inconvenient to revoke them without cause. If the name is changed and re-registered, they will inevitably be subjected to various criticisms and may not be granted approval. New ones will be difficult to establish, and old ones may be forced to dissolve. Overseas Chinese merchants will have no possibility of unity, and the contracts and properties held under the (Malay transliteration name) will become invalid at the same time, resulting in considerable losses. We believe that the government cherishes overseas Chinese compatriots with utmost care. Previously, the association telegraphed to request aid for the Kunming fire, and the National Government immediately ordered officials to provide comfort and instructed the Ministry of Finance and the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to telegraph 100,000 yuan, and the Relief Committee telegraphed 10,000 yuan. The overseas Chinese community is deeply grateful. If we allow overseas Chinese Chambers of Commerce to be dissolved due to this insignificant matter of name, it will not only contradict the original intention of the legislation but also be unbearable for all of you at this conference. Therefore, we earnestly implore you to consider that overseas Chinese compatriots have consistently loved the country and the party for a long time. They participated in the Northern Expedition and the Eastern Campaign. Please grant the motion to amend Article 41 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Chamber of Commerce Law (Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce will be renamed Overseas Chinese Chambers of Commerce under this law) so that the Overseas Chinese General Chambers of Commerce can continue to use their old names. Then, overseas Chinese compatriots will feel the government's kindness and your generosity, and they will cooperate more vigorously with the domestic industrial and commercial circles to the end. We earnestly present this matter to you and wish you all the best. Overseas Chinese Federation, respectfully, Jiang Yin."

Chambers of Commerce of Various Counties in Jiangsu Request Prompt Discussion of

Nanjing, 3rd: The chambers of commerce of Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Dongtai, Haimen, Taixian, Jiangdu, Kunshan, Wuhuai, Wujiang, Qidong, Wuxi, Taixing, Ying, Nantong, Liyang, Jiangyin, Xinghua, Danyang, Gaoyou, Liuhe, Jiangpu, Suqian, Qingpu, Jingjiang, Peixian, Nanhui, Chuansha, Yizheng, Yihe, Jiading, Fengxian, Suining, Jintan, Changshu, Siyang, Pixian, Jurong, Yancheng, etc., sent a telegram to the secretariat of the Industrial and Commercial Conference, which was forwarded to all members, stating that the issue of changing commercial accounting dates is urgent and chaotic in various industries in Jiangsu Province and Jiangbei. They requested that this case be discussed in advance and that the end date be set as the sixteenth day of the second month of the lunar calendar of the following year, according to the methods used in Jiangsu Province, so that the overall situation will not be in danger.

Opening of Cotton Industry Exhibition 122

At 2:00 PM on November 3rd, the opening ceremony of the Cotton Industry Exhibition at the National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce was held. Over two hundred representatives from various government agencies and commercial organizations, as well as guests, attended. The Vice Minister of Industry and Commerce, Zhou Yue, presided over the ceremony and delivered a speech, stating that he was honored by the presence of all sectors at the opening of today's Cotton Industry Exhibition. The purpose of the exhibition is to promote domestic goods. The Japanese residing in China still use goods dried in the sun, which shows that promoting domestic goods is the most important thing today. It is not that the Chinese do not love domestic goods, but because domestic goods are not refined and pursue luxury, so they prefer to use foreign goods. Now, domestic goods have been improved and progressed, and everyone should emulate the enthusiasm of the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, and Japan in loving and using domestic goods to promote and use domestic goods. Only then can there be hope for the recovery of China's economy. One more thing, Indian silk is a product of domestic silk factories, but because Chinese people like to use foreign goods, this silk is named after foreign names. From now on, it is hoped that the society will use domestic silk and that domestic silk factories will not name Chinese silk goods with foreign terms. Next, Li Chongshi, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, and Xu Jianhong, representative of the National Government, delivered speeches. Next, Zhang Wohua, Vice Minister of the Ministry of the Interior, and others also gave speeches.

Index of Proposals

Second Group 124

Glimpses of Proposals

Opinions and Six Proposals on Developing Overseas Chinese Industry and Commerce 127

(Proposal | Chen Anren, Representative of the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission)

The state of China's national economy and production has fallen into an extremely difficult situation urgently awaiting relief. This is something we cannot deny. From the perspective of the significance of the progress of the National Revolution, China will not have the opportunity to improve its national economy and production situation unless it completely eliminates the last remaining warlords in the North as soon as possible. From the perspective of the development of the national organism, China will not have a place for the progress of its national economy and production situation unless it restores social order in the shortest possible time, unifies the divided situation, and pacifies the phenomenon of war and turmoil that has lasted for more than a decade. Therefore, in today's terms, the major premise for improving and advancing the national economy and production situation is how to quickly complete the National Revolution, eliminate the warlords who hinder the economy and production, and how to quickly unify China's situation and eliminate all reactionaries. The simplest expectation is no less. However, China's current national economy and production situation is hindered and oppressed by foreign economic forces, making it even more difficult to rise. Therefore, in developing the national economy and production situation, on the negative side, it is necessary to eliminate the economic status of imperialism in China. According to foreign investment in China, the amount is about 2.5 billion yuan, of which Japan accounts for the largest investment, followed by the United Kingdom, and then the United States. According to a 1924 customs survey, there are 4,278 Japanese commercial firms in China, 726 British firms, and 470 American firms. Except for the United States, British and Japanese investment in China is mostly in commerce. British investment in China, including shipping, the cigarette industry, mining, banking, electricity, and other industries, amounts to approximately 43.7 million pounds, excluding loans for postal administration, railways, and other projects. Japanese investment in China in railways, transportation, warehouses, banks, textiles, agriculture, forestry, manufacturing, electricity, civil engineering, and other industries amounts to approximately 1.89 billion yuan. American investment in China amounts to approximately 147 million yuan, and the purchase of bonds in the Far East amounts to approximately 100 million yuan. Other expropriations of concessions, leased territories, banks, etc., are difficult to calculate. Furthermore, according to 192x statistics, British trade with China amounts to 319,594,403 pounds. Japanese trade with China, such as cotton textiles, cotton yarn, sugar, porcelain, paper, etc., according to 1929 statistics, amounts to 330,820,000 taels. American trade with China has been vigorously increasing in recent years. According to a 1917 survey, American trade with China accounted for 12 percent of China's foreign trade, and it has increased even more in recent years. Among the goods shipped to China, kerosene, tobacco, hardware, machinery, timber, and flour account for the most important positions. German trade with China has also made rapid progress in recent years. The damage to the national economy and national financial resources caused by the decline in foreign trade and the erosion of China by foreign goods is incalculable. Therefore, the development of China's industry and commerce cannot be achieved without eliminating the economic aggressive forces of foreign countries in China. Otherwise, trade with China has become a blood-sucking ghost that will die from exhaustion if not from consumption. Based on the current situation in China and the economic aggression of foreign countries against China, there is a way to save China from danger and recover the hardships of society and people's livelihood. What is this? From us, we further observe the current situation inside China. Due to the barrenness of land and the low yield, the increasing number of disaster areas, and the reduction of farmers, various reasons affect the panic of farmers' associations. The average annual import of agricultural products from the first year of the Republic of China to the ninth year is about 50 million yuan, and it has increased even more in recent years. Due to the decreasing agricultural production, other industrial and commercial industries have fallen into a state of decline. Now, our people feel that if we do not develop industry and commerce, we will not be able to survive in the world. The internal and external situation of China is already like this. Will we procrastinate, perfunctorily, and live in complacency to maintain the remaining situation, or will we rise up and strive for the final effort and struggle? We observe that after Germany's defeat in the war, not only was its politics destroyed, but its economy was even more severely damaged. After the war, reparations of 1.25 billion marks had to be paid out every year. Germany suffered this severe blow and vigorously reformed its domestic industry and commerce. As a result, the strong monopolization and rationalization of the industry came into being, and Germany's economic situation gradually changed, the productivity gradually increased, and the national livelihood gradually improved. After the revolution, Russia's economy fell into

A Word of Wisdom 128

— Zeng Jun

Too much closeness easily breeds rifts. Once affection breaks down and people hate each other, it's better than being strangers. Therefore, the friendship of gentlemen is as light as water.

An honest and sincere person, once misled into evil ways, will be beyond redemption.

Overemphasizing science makes life feel dry and dull; overemphasizing spirituality makes life even more lifeless.

Etiquette is a large curtain. Although one knows that it conceals some ugly things and is not really clean, to remove it would reveal the ugly deeds of society, which would be even more unbearable.

Without flattering, one cannot get food to eat; without boasting, one cannot gain people's trust.

Those who force people into despair and discouragement are as guilty as murderers.

It's not good if a woman is not beautiful because no one will love her; it's also not good if a woman is beautiful because everyone will fight for her.

An ugly person should be dignified to slightly hide their ugliness; a beautiful person can be more beautiful if they are dignified. As for those who wear makeup and make seductive gestures, they are all playthings of the world.

The endpoint of love is carnal desire. There is no pure spiritual love without special circumstances.

Hope with determination is ambition; hope that benefits oneself and harms others is ambition; hoping for something that one knows cannot be achieved is delusion. Ambition is necessary for ambition; there is no harm in having it, but delusion should not be had.

In Memory of Mr. Tian Tong, a Pioneer of the Kuomintang 129

— Zhang Jinguang

Mr. Tian, whose given name was Tong and courtesy name was Ziqin, was a pioneer of the Chinese Kuomintang from Jinchun, Hubei. He was chivalrous by nature and possessed the virtues of ancient gentlemen. His learning was profound, and both Chinese and foreign people who had the opportunity to hear his words and observe his demeanor admired and respected him. He had great ambitions from a young age. At a time when the Qing Dynasty was in danger and the political system was disintegrating, Mr. Tian was indignant at the defeat of the national cause and even more saddened by the suffering of the people. He believed that the world was in turmoil and did not know where it was going. If things continued like this, the country would cease to be a country. Therefore, he advocated reform and revolution and the establishment of a republic. As a result, he was hated by the Qing court, which secretly ordered his arrest, and there was no place for Mr. Tian to stand in the country. So he went to the East to seek further education and met the late Premier in Tokyo. They declared their goals of saving the country and confided in each other. They were overjoyed and inexplicably happy. They discussed revolutionary principles day and night and founded the Alliance to overthrow the Qing court and build a republic. Mr. Tian and the other members of the association traveled around to promote their ideas. Although they suffered repeated failures, they persevered and opened up the stubborn national customs of our country for thousands of years, leading them to the road of revolution. When the Wuchang Uprising broke out and the Republic of China was founded, Mr. Tian was appointed as the Hubei Pacification Commissioner and other positions. His political achievements were remarkable, and his contributions were immense. His moral integrity was especially beyond the reach of ordinary people. Because the two cases of imperial system and bribery in elections were successively multiplied, although there were many councilors at that time, they were hesitant and dared not speak out. Only Mr. Tian resolutely advocated the proposal of the National Assembly in the South. Later, he led the public to the South. Mr. Tian's power was great. Mr. Tian treated people with kindness and generosity, but when it came to the great righteousness, he also argued with his strict teachers and good friends, without any hesitation. When the late Premier proposed the Ronggong plan, Mr. Tian strongly opposed it. Knowing that it could not be reversed, he flicked his sleeves and left, saying to the late Premier, "The two of us are the only confidants. Since our political views are different, it is absolutely difficult to work together again. Private friendship will remain intact. From now on, I will regard you as a lifelong friend." Therefore, he resigned and retired to Songbin. At that time, I looked up to the Yuan Yue and personally received his teachings. The boundless clear waves benefited me infinitely. Mr. Ying told me, "Revolutionary youths should have a particularly calm and determined attitude and an uncompromising spirit. Even if they suffer repeated failures, they must not be pessimistic. This is a necessary situation in the evolution of the revolution. They must cultivate their spirit and learning and wait for the opportunity to rise again, so as not to fail as revolutionary youths." His words were reasonable and will last forever. In recent years, although Mr. has been living in seclusion in Songyun, his heart of worrying about the country has never been able to abandon himself. Therefore, he used his lifelong learning and experience to express his great views and founded the Taiping Magazine for people to refer to. The content is very rich, and the arguments are all bright and grand. Readers have praised and admired him endlessly. To speak for the world is what it means. Alas, I was hoping that Mr. Yuan Yuan would write and feed me new knowledge, and I was especially hoping that he would rise again in Dongshan and plan for development. Why did God not leave him behind and take my teacher away so quickly? Alas, Dao is too great to contain, and talent is difficult to use. I mourn for Mr.'s misfortune and grieve for the future of China.

Cat and Dog Barber Shops in New York 130

— Shuiqiu

Western women's fondness for raising cats and dogs has become a common practice. Wealthy families even spend huge sums to acquire exotic breeds to show off to relatives and friends. Therefore, the value of cats and dogs in Western society is indeed higher than elsewhere. Speculative merchants and those who raise dogs have opened cat and dog barber shops to specialize in bathing cats and dogs and profit from them. Recently, the opening of such barber shops along Broadway Road in New York has become numerous. There are two ways to bathe cats and dogs, and the prices are also different. One is dry cleaning, which only uses disinfectant mixed with bleaching powder, costing about half a dollar to one and a half dollars each time. The other is wet cleaning, which is the same as washing cats and dogs at home, costing about forty cents to seventy or eighty cents each time. European and American women are afraid of hard work and like leisure. Therefore, those who have cats and dogs all bring them to this kind of barber shop to wash them, and cat and dog barbers make a lot of money. There are also such businesses in Paris, London, and other cities, and dog doctors also operate this business a lot. I know that in the near future, such businesses will also be discovered in Shanghai.

An Investigation Record of Shipu Port in Ermen Bay 131

— Xu Xinfu

Shipu Port is located in the northeast of Sanmen Bay, belonging to Xiangshan County, Zhejiang Province. It is an important fish market. It is 180 miles away from Dinghai, 240 miles away from Zhenhai, 170 miles away from Haimen, and 350 miles away from Wenzhou. The waterway has two gates, east and west. The west Sanmen (Xiaosanmen) is winding and shallow, and the east Tongwa Gate waterway is narrow and winding, with strong currents. Boats must wait for the tide to be level to enter and exit the lower bay. The two ports of Dongmen are narrow and have many reefs, and no one dares to try to travel. The southwest side of the city is deep, four or five to more than ten fathoms, where small ships can dock. The larger ships can also dock on the left and right of Manshan or west of Jinqi Gate, but when encountering the southeast wind, the waves are very large. The tide is high at nine and a quarter during the new and full moon. The high tide can be two fathoms, and the low tide is also more than one fathom. The larger sand reefs are the Laohu Reef at the east entrance of the Shumengang Port, which is hidden when the tide rises. The Linmengang Port has four reefs near the two mountain mouths. The Xiabawan Port also has several reefs at the east entrance. There are many reefs on the southeast side of Danantian Island. The larger islands are Dongmen, Dafu, Daguzhongjie, Yutang, Changkeng, Waidan Shuangshan, Beihezhonghe, Nanhe, Pingfeng, Lianchuitongtou, Huangzhitan, Tontouniluo, Nantian Nanshan, Yancanshan Danshuimen, and other islands. Among them, the Sanmen Mountain Island is located at the mouth of Sanmen Bay, and the terrain is particularly dangerous. The city and town are built on the mountain, and the city is densely populated. The southeast coastal area is named Yancangqian, which is a prosperous fish market. Ten miles to the northeast is Changguo Weiwei, half of which is barren. There are few houses in the north, but the streets are wide, and five horses can enter side by side. It was once an important town on the coast where the commander was stationed. The old school field outside the south gate is quite wide, separated from the Nanhui Mountain on the opposite bank. The east gate of the south side of the city has been dilapidated for a long time and has recently become a gathering place for fishermen. It is actually a fishing village. At the end of the east side of the island, Mentou has a lamp tower built by the Ren Xiaohe brothers. The inscription on the stele in front of the tower was written by Master Yu Changlin. The guest room also has many ink marks by Master Yu. Looking far away, the sea is wide and the sky is clear. It is a summer resort here, even better than Guling and Mogan. The main local products are fish and salt, followed by mountain potatoes, rice, and valleys. However, the mountains are barren and abandoned, which is a pity. If scientific new methods can be adopted to engage in agricultural and forestry industries, the future prospects are immeasurable. Moreover, this port is surrounded by mountains, and the terrain is majestic. The route is tortuous, which is the hub between Shanghai and Hong Kong in Zhejiang. Choosing a place on the north and south banks of the port can build a shipyard, which can be rectified and used as a resting place for naval cruisers. Is it just a fishing port?

Qiuling's Sayings 132

— Fengjia

Water caltrop is a fine fruit of autumn, originally written as 蔆. The Shuowen says (蔆 is also called 芰 in Chu, 薢茩 in Qin, also called water chestnut, also called shaguo. The Wulin Record (the four-cornered is called 芰, the two-cornered is called water caltrop, its flowers bloom at night and close during the day, and move with the moon like the sunflower moves with the sun). Most of the products in Wuxia are four-cornered, but they are also commonly called water caltrop, and no one calls them 芰. However, Qu Dao, who loves 芰, was seen early in ancient books, so China has 芕 since ancient times. The different names of 芰 and water caltrop, but in fact of the same kind, can also be seen.

The method of planting water caltrops is to harvest old water caltrops after Chongyang Festival and soak them in the river for two or three months to germinate, then sprinkle them into the pond. The stems and ends emerge with leaves, slightly triangular, exposed to the water surface, with floating sacs on the petioles. When the leaves are abundant, there are duckweeds mixed in, which are removed. In summer, small white flowers bloom with four petals. The fruit has four corners, three corners, and two corners, so it is called water caltrop. It is either green or red, both raw and ripe are suitable. The ripe ones are soft and sweet, and the raw and tender ones are peeled and eaten, crisp like sad pears. Simmering with water caltrop white meat slices is especially delicious as a suocuan.

In my hometown's lakes and ponds, many small water caltrops are planted. The ones with sharp corners are commonly called touch-mouth water caltrops, and the ones with blunt corners are commonly called bald water caltrops. There are also reddish ones with a larger shape, commonly called water red water caltrops. Chen Yaozu's so-called pile of ripe water caltrops with rouge corners is sung about here. Every time the group orders young girls to ride wooden round barrels, stirring the water and flowing into the depths of the water caltrop bushes, their slender hands and green onions pick them one by one, then light songs and beautiful sentences are sent with the wind from a distance. Looking at the waves and figures from afar, it is like a wonderful water caltrop picking picture. Emperor Wu of Liang's poem says (Jiangnan girls' pearl wrists are amazing, cinnamon oars leisurely sing and pick water caltrops). Jiang Hong's water caltrop picking song says (the wind gives birth to green leaves and gathers waves, the purple stems bloom, containing flowers and fruits, waiting for a beautiful woman to come). This scene and this feeling are like paintings.

Between August and September, fresh water caltrops are sold on the market streets. Men, women, old and young, are not one of them, borrowing the opportunity to earn a small profit, which is also a speculative business for ordinary hawkers. Only in Pingwang Town in my town is it a different scene. The little family is beautiful and moving, carrying a basket and weighing scales, tripping through tea houses and taverns, often selling water caltrops in a charming voice and smiling and attracting people again and again. Customers with a drunkard's intention often welcome them. Life is quite bad, and the dragon is also a romance.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (72) 133

— Linghua

On the seventh day, I arrived at Namyo and stayed at a Yunnan-owned inn. I asked about the rules. One meal costs half a yuan, and two meals cost one yuan. The room fee is not included. The meat and vegetables are very good, but I don't like them. However, the room is just a shed. There are many people, mountain slopes, forests, streams, waterfalls, and British houses and companies on the top of the mountain. The electric lights illuminate the night. When arriving at the station, the disease is first checked, and the ticket can be entered. Namyo is just a mountain village. There are restaurants in the stations. Its habits are the same as Penang. There are also such hotels in Penang, a large port, which do not count the money but only calculate the food. It is also strange. I once visited a friend whose residence was on Huoche Tou Street. I asked about the price. My friend said, "One night's room is one yuan, and each meal is two and a half jiao." But the room costs one yuan for ten days and one yuan for a month. I was very surprised and saw that the room could accommodate eight people, but in fact it could only accommodate two or three people. I am now traveling everywhere to avoid countless societies that cannot be judged by ordinary theories. Different places have different rights and wrongs.

There are Ban Yi people here, who are a kind of Burmese people with different languages, as well as mountain people and wild people. Men must carry knives when they go out, and women carry a hoe to trade goods. The women's clothes are beautiful, and the men are also handsome and not very black. The girls who are not married have short hair and are lively and strong, but unfortunately they are not educated. Yunnan people who go home pass through the settlements of mountain people. Single people are often imprisoned and sacrificed by them. It is a custom. In the Spring and Autumn Period of our country, Song Xiangtu

Basha still held Zeng Zi to sacrifice to ghosts. It is not easy to discuss the height of culture. How can this small nation be blamed? There are tailor shops run by Kalla people. Kalla people are a kind of Indian people. They hang a large water pipe in front of them, three feet high and four feet long. It is also the largest one I have seen in various places in Guangdong, Guangxi, and Southeast Asia.

The Chinese nation has failed to become the greatest nation. Without the support of politics, its power has spread to five continents. Although it is weak now, it is still conceited and often calls others ghosts. Westerners call them hairy ghosts. Kalla people call them black ghosts. The Ban Yi people call them Ban Yi ghosts. The Burmese call them old Burmese. The old means stupid and dull. To this day, it is still like the heavenly Chinese stomach, which can also be comforting. A certain Liu from Yunnan talked about going to the dog country on the border between India and Myanmar. I cannot say its name. The name in the local language of the dog country is the name added by us Chinese. They do not call it dog, but call it dog country. Its location is in southwestern Myanmar. It takes a total of 23 days to travel. It takes four days by boat from Vancheng to Mengzhua, then four days by boat to Jilairin. Then go southwest for ten days to the mountains on the Indian border, which is the dog country. It is very poor and the food is only half-ripe taro corn. The people have no clothes, but the weather is not cold. The frost is an inch deep. It belongs to the British camp. Liu went to transport goods by horse for the British. The country likes Chinese people very much and hates British people. During the European War, the British levied a tax of two yuan per person, otherwise they had to join the army. They also asked for six animals. The locals hated them and often ambushed in the forest to shoot British people. There are also Chinese people who work as carpenters. Liu could not remember the original name of the country.

— Liu Haisu

Italian Tour Diary

(3) Rome, Ten Days (6)

— La ville eternelle, the Immortal City

June 1st, Spanish Masterpiece Exhibition and Sun-Drenched Modern Art Exhibition

Kawai Gyokudo, Komuro Suisho, Yamanouchi Tamon, etc. are students of the Southern School; Araki Mujin, Gen Shunkyo, and Domoto Insho are pure academy styles; Kojori Tomone and Kaburaki Kiyokata can be considered regular Japanese paintings, but they are just thickly applying powder and stealing the end skills of the Tang people. In terms of propaganda skills, their efforts and sincere attitude are worth admiring. From the perspective of the meaning of the content of the work, it is very superficial and annoying. The superficial beauty and frivolous attitude are like butterflies floating on spring wildflowers. It is said that their government allocated a huge sum of money for this meeting in Italy. The rich man Okura Kihachiro also donated 100,000 US dollars and invited the writer Yokoyama Taikan to come to Rome with a dozen of his disciples to respond. It can be seen that this is a major event that the Japanese pay close attention to. They are promoting culture to the outside world and raising their international status, posing as one of the so-called five major powers in the world. Every year they hold meetings in Paris and London, and it is always so exaggerated. Speaking of this, I can't help but imitate the tone of Shirakaba Itoku and say口:

The Japanese always want to show off their art everywhere. However, hasn't there always been no real painting in Japan? Isn't there also no real sculpture? What seems to be painting and what seems to be sculpture are just foreign ideas obtained from the Chinese. In fact, they are borrowings and revisions. To issue thorough efforts and culture, the corresponding vitality and foundation are not enough, so they can only fly out like butterflies, small and agile, and dazzling.

Ah, forgive them a little bit. There is no soil in their flowerpots. However, Europeans are generally deceived. You hear us traveling all over Europe, whether talking about art or literature, we always recommend the Japanese as the representatives of the East. In their minds, there is naturally no shadow of China at all, unless a very small number of specialized scholars know that the source of Eastern culture is in China. Don't say that. How about our Chinese ourselves? Even these small abilities and small agility don't have the basic ability to improve and have no interest. They only know how to sell the glory of their ancestors' legacy and have no reflection at all. They are completely depraved.

Double Palace Silk Factory Also Announced Closure 148

There are a total of 106 single and double palace silk factories in this port, all of which are members of the Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association. Because the silk sales in Europe and the United States are not good, the silk factory's business has suffered losses. On the 19th of last month, an interim emergency meeting of the industry was held, and it was unanimously decided to suspend business and wait for government relief. As of the 31st of last month, all silk factories in Shanghai have been shut down. There are a total of 7 double palace silk factories in the Shanghai port, all of which have joined the Industry Association General Assembly resolution and must be observed. Therefore, the seven double palace silk factories, including Hongshunlun, Xinlun, Jinglun, Fulun, Ruilun, Jinlun, and Dalun, all 　 stopped working at the end of last month.

The Oil Market Asphalt Market is Firm 153

This year's asphalt inventory is unusually dry, and the Jingzhou oil that is sold in the market is also lacking in goods. Although there are goods arriving in the market, they are all sent by the Tongzhou and Tianjin gangs. The transaction price is 16 liang 6 qian for the three constant heavy Jing and 15 liang for the Tianjin market. The Macheng oil still has 1,000 pieces in stock, and the wholesale price is 16 liang 2 qian to 4 qian. There is still more than a month before the new time, and the market is unusually firm. The current market price opened by this city line yesterday was 21 liang 6 qian for the famous heavy Jing, 22 liang 5 qian for the three constant heavy Jing, 21 liang 3 qian for the high miscellaneous heavy Jing, 20 liang and 8 qian for the sharp flat Jing, 20 liang and 6 qian for the high flat Jing, and 20 liang and 5 qian for the sharp Macheng.

Sichuan occupied new goods (also known as white 　) have already debuted, but there are few arrivals in Shanghai. The old goods guest plate was 108 liang, and the new goods opened at 107 liang. The Price of Hardware and Bamboo Joint Steel Declines Daily] 155

Although the recent trading of bamboo joint steel is very active, the market price is only showing a downward trend due to oversupply. The current market is estimated at only ninety-five or ninety-six taels. It is said that there are still few buyers. According to news from the construction industry, a large quantity of this product will arrive this week, and there are fears that the market price will continue to fall.

Qing Lead from Ting Province is Now Available

The source of Hunan Qing lead has been cut off for a long time, so merchants who generally need this product in the market are eagerly awaiting it. Recently, shipments from Hunan have gradually begun to arrive in Shanghai, so those who need to purchase it are making large-scale special purchases. Therefore, in the past few days, two to three thousand dan have been shipped for export. The price is fourteen taels per dan. It is said that another large batch is arriving soon, so the market outlook is bound to be lively.

Local News

Chen Ying Shi Memorial Tower 160

Completion ceremony held at 10:00 AM yesterday, with deeply sorrowful speeches from Mayor Zhang and others. Yesterday at 10:00 AM, the completion ceremony for the memorial tower of the late General Chen Ying Shi, Military Governor of Shanghai, was held at the triangular area between Ximen Fang Xie Road and Zhonghua Road in this city. The streets around Ximen were bustling with traffic, marking a grand occasion. Details of the day are recorded separately below. The memorial tower was built with funds raised by Chairman Chiang, Mayor Zhang, and Mr. Huang Yingbai. The tower's appearance is completely in the Chinese style, with an overall height of eighty feet. The highest point is shaped like a giant cauldron, gilded in gold. The entire structure is constructed of steel and reinforced concrete, with an exterior resembling natural stone, making it exceptionally majestic. Inside, a spiral staircase allows visitors to ascend and admire the surrounding scenery, making it an unprecedented structure in this city.

Attendees and Guests: Those who participated in the ceremony included Mr. Huang Yingbai, representative of National Government Chairman Chiang; Mr. Jiao Yitang, representative of Legislative Yuan President Hu; Mayor Zhang; Central Committee members Li Shizeng and Li Liejun, as well as He Yaozu, Liu Jiwen, Yu Hongjun, Tang Naikang, Zhu Yan, Pan Gongzhan, Shen Yi, Yuan Liang, Hu Hongji, Xu Pei璜, Huang Boqiao, Xi Dingmo, Sun Baorong, Xu Weizhen, Ren Guangyu, Chen Xunyong, Yang Hu, Su Xianyang, Wu Kaixian, Zhu Yingpeng, Wang Yansong, Fan Zhengbo, Tong Xingbai, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Guo Chengen, Chen Shiguang, Wu Zhenxiu, Chu Fucheng, Xu Xiuzhi, Zhou Peizhen, Yin Ru, Wen Lanting, Yuan Ludeng, and foreign guests such as Kikuchi Ryoichi, totaling over a thousand people.

Family Members of Martyr Chen: In addition to the guests, family members of Mr. Chen Yingqi, including Ying Shi's wife Chen Lanshi, Chen Qinshi, Chen Lifu, Chen Ganfu, Chen Zhenfu, Chen Qianfu, Chen Hanfu, and Chen Xizeng, totaling over twenty people, were also present.

Order of the Completion Ceremony: (1) Opening—all stand at attention; (2) Music; (3) Singing of the Party anthem; (4) Bowing three times to the Party flag, national flag, and the portrait of the Leader; (5) Chairman respectfully reads the Leader's will; (6) Silence; (7) Chairman delivers the opening address; (8) Music; (9) Unveiling ceremony; (10) Speeches; (11) Music; (12) Adjournment.

Mayor Zhang's Speech: After the opening, Chairman Mayor Zhang delivered a speech, briefly stating: "Today is November 3rd, the nineteenth year of the Republic of China. On this day nineteen years ago, Mr. Chen Ying Shi, following the Leader's plan, led our revolutionary comrades, disregarding the sacrifice of their lives, to bravely restore Shanghai and establish the foundation for the revolution. His great achievements, broadly speaking, are related to the Republic of China; narrowly speaking, they are related to Shanghai. How deeply felt is this relationship since Mr. Ying Shi's martyrdom. Since Mr. Ying Shi's martyrdom, we have wanted to have something in Shanghai to commemorate him, to serve as a reminder. It was not until the nineteenth year of the Republic of China that we were able to build this small memorial tower for Mr. Chen in Shanghai. Looking back now, amidst our joy, there is infinite sorrow and infinite shame. Today, you gentlemen share the same sentiment and have graced us with your presence to participate in the ceremony. Several of you have come from afar, from Nanjing, Suzhou, and Hangzhou. Your spirit of admiring martyrs is particularly admirable. Mr. Chiang Kai-shek originally planned to attend the ceremony but was unable to come due to pressing matters. He specially requested Mr. Huang Yingbai to deliver a speech on his behalf, so today we will also ask Mr. Huang to share his thoughts. As for the origin of building this memorial tower, Mr. Huang and I reported on it when the groundbreaking ceremony was held on May 18th, so there is no need to repeat it. All the engineering was completely entrusted to Mr. Shen Junjunyi, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works, and Mr. Dong Dayou. Mr. Xue Jun Cixin supervised the construction on our behalf. Since the groundbreaking, everything has proceeded according to the scheduled plan, so we were able to complete it today on the scheduled date. The tower is eighty feet tall, and most of it is in the Chinese architectural style, but it also incorporates foreign architectural elements. The materials are almost all domestic goods. Entering the tower door, you can climb to the top along the stairs. If you use a surveying instrument at the top of the tower to test it, you can see that the tower is very straight and has no slight inclination. It can be considered the tallest building among the public buildings in this city, and it cost only over 10,000 yuan. When we ascend this tower, we can not only commemorate the martyrs but also have a clear view of the entire city. It is not without benefit to municipal administration. Among the guests today, there are many old friends or colleagues of Mr. Ying Shi. Seeing this scene, they must have many thoughts. I don't need to say more. Please express your thoughts to commemorate him."

Huang Yingbai's Speech: After Mayor Zhang's speech, Mr. Huang, former mayor, representing Chairman Chiang, delivered a speech, briefly stating: "The greatness of Mr. Ying Shi's character and the hardships of creating the Republic of China were described in detail by me when this memorial tower's foundation stone laying ceremony was held on May 18th. Today, at this opening ceremony, it was originally planned for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to attend and deliver a speech, so I did not prepare to speak. Unexpectedly, yesterday I received a telegram from Chairman Chiang stating that he was unable to arrive as scheduled due to matters and asked me to deliver a speech on his behalf, so I cannot but repeat a few words. However, since I am speaking on behalf of him, then what I say can only be taken as Chairman Chiang Kai-shek speaking here. This memorial tower was selected to have its foundation laid on the day Mr. Ying Shi opposed the imperial system and sacrificed himself for the country. It was also selected to have its opening ceremony on the day Mr. Ying Shi was almost in danger but restored Shanghai. This kind of commemorative method cannot but be said to contain a profound meaning. What is the meaning? It is to let the gloriously dead know that the martyrs did not create the Republic of China easily, to constantly observe things and feel the need to continue to work hard to complete the martyrs' unfulfilled wishes. It is neither to comfort the private feelings of one or two people nor merely to enhance the appearance of Shanghai. However, what are the unfulfilled wishes of Mr. Ying Shi? I dare to give a simple answer: under the Leader's guidance, strive to realize the Three Principles of the People in China. I still remember that Mr. Ying Shi, during the secret work era, once discussed the Three Principles of the People with his comrades. He said that since it is called the Three Principles of the People, we must first understand that the word 'people' refers to all the people. If it does not include all the people, it is not enough to speak of nationalism. If a part of the people occupies a special position and exercises special power, it is not enough to speak of democracy. If a few people live and the majority die or wither, it is not enough to speak of people's livelihood. This is one saying. He also said that nationalism is the ultimate goal of our party, and democracy and people's livelihood are the only ways to achieve the goal. This is another saying. We can know the location of Mr. Ying Shi's unfulfilled wishes based on his two sayings during his lifetime. Before the Xinhai Revolution, the party's ideology was not widely spread in the country, so at the time of the Xinhai Revolution, most people saw that nationalism was listed first in the party's ideology and thought that nationalism was only the solution to the Manchu-Han problem. I do not know that our party's nationalism is by no means so narrow. The Leader's will clearly states: 'To seek freedom and equality for the Chinese nation,' so nationalism is actually the ultimate goal of our party. However, to seek national freedom in the international arena, we must first seek the establishment of democracy and the prosperity of people's livelihood within the country. The establishment of democracy is the cause of political progress, and the prosperity of people's livelihood is the result of economic development. There has never been a nation with chaotic politics and backward economy that can seek freedom and equality in the international arena. Therefore, Mr. Ying Shi said that democracy and people's livelihood are the only ways to achieve the goal. Now, let me explain the three meanings of nationalism, democracy, and people's livelihood separately: (1) Nationalism: Mr. Ying Shi said that if it does not include all the people, it is not enough to speak of nationalism. How can all the people be united? From a political and legal point of view, it is necessary to maintain the peace and unity of the country. From a social point of view, it is necessary to cultivate the spirit of love and sincerity. The former is the policy of the current government, and the latter is the late Leader's teachings. Following this teaching and based on this policy, we can proceed, so that in the villages and communities, there will be the beauty of mutual friendship and assistance, watching out for each other, and helping each other in times of illness. In the country, we can achieve the effect of unity from top to bottom, with one heart and one mind, striving together for this ultimate goal. Being able to be friends and help each other will never lead to mutual harm and trouble. To put it in today's common language, it is the theory of mutual assistance. Being able to have the same heart and mind will never lead to diverging paths. To put it in today's common language, it is the theory of cooperation. I deeply hope that the whole country will support the policy of unity and peace with the spirit of love and sincerity. Let the past be like yesterday's death, and let the future be like today's birth. I am willing to encourage all my comrades together. (2) Democracy: Mr. Ying Shi said that it is not enough to speak of democracy if people in special positions exercise special powers. In a country, having special positions and special powers is the greatest misfortune and the greatest danger. This great misfortune and this danger are not only suffered by those who are not special, but those who are special will also personally suffer. The nobles of the former Qing Dynasty and the warlords of the Republic of China are proof of this. The people of the whole country can be roughly divided into four categories. Guanzi said that scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants are the four classes of people in a country. If one of the four is missing, the country cannot stand. It is evident that the ancients had the theory of equality among the four classes of people. If the four classes of people do not have their own foundations and do not have equal opportunities for development, it is not enough to speak of establishing a country. I hope that during the period of political tutelage

Right: Zhang Qun (Center): Ying Shi's Wife (Left): Huang Fu (Our Newspaper) 161

First pay attention to this and gradually cultivate the habit and experience of equal participation in politics among the four classes of people so that the principle of democracy can be fully realized. (3) People's Livelihood: Mr. Ying Shi said that it is not enough to speak of people's livelihood if a few people live and the majority die. To seek the livelihood of the majority, we must ask the majority to move forward together on the path of economic construction. The obstacles to the first step of economic construction are the incitement of the Communist Party, the disturbance of bandits, irregular actions among groups, and the undisciplined behavior of the military and political circles. The government should, of course, bear full responsibility for removing these obstacles. At the same time, the elements of economic construction, the way to work diligently and live frugally, cannot but be expected from the joint efforts of all the people. Those who are diligent are hardworking, and those who live frugally are thrifty. Being hardworking and thrifty is enough to speak of economic construction. Otherwise, if they are lazy at work and compete in luxury, not only will the principle of people's livelihood be far from the topic, but the impact will induce the economic invasion policies of countries around the world to penetrate deeply into the country and cause disharmony in the world. This is most regrettable. Today, taking the opportunity of the completion ceremony of the Chen Ying Shi Memorial Tower, and also at a time when the whole country is rejoicing in peace and the military affairs of the last act of unity, which has suffered the most hardship and made the greatest sacrifices, has completely ended, I do not mind taking the time to tell you all my innermost feelings.

Now that I have finished speaking on behalf of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, I want to return to Huang Yingbai and talk about the previous section of the speech on behalf of him was not because Chairman Chiang had telegrammed me, but it was not a fiction of my own. I know that the history of the combination of Chiang Kai-shek and Ying Shi and my usual discussions with Chiang Kai-shek know that what he wants to say today is roughly the same. Why? The prerequisite for nationalism is that all the people have the spirit of love and sincerity, and Chiang Kai-shek has often inscribed the four characters of 'love and sincerity' when he inscribed words for people in recent years. This proves that it is not my fiction. First, the prerequisite for democracy is that the four classes of people are equal, and there are no special positions and no special powers in the whole country. This was recently said with emotion by Chiang Kai-shek when he returned from the battlefield and held a commemorative week in the capital. This proves that it is not my fiction. Second, the prerequisite for the meaning of people's livelihood is to remove the obstacles to economic construction, and Chiang Kai-shek began to clear the Communists after he established the capital in Nanjing. After returning from the battlefield this time, he also paid attention to suppressing bandits. This also proves that it is not my fiction. Third, I also remember that in the winter of the year of Jiazi, when I was in charge of politics in Beiping, Chiang Kai-shek sent a telegram from Guangzhou, briefly stating: 'The political situation in the north has changed suddenly, and your brother expected that your brother must have participated. The telegrams sent in recent days to eliminate the war and clean up the old palace are indeed what your brother did. Hearing this, I was moved to tears. Your brother is now doing his best to train soldiers in Guangzhou, so that the national revolution can be completed and the Leader's ideology can be realized and Ying's brother's unfulfilled wishes can be extended, then our Qi's heart and traces can be made clear to the world.' Therefore, I dare to believe that Chiang Kai-shek's spirit for the party and the country has been the same for decades. When Shanghai people warmly praised the world's talents during the Xinhai Restoration, Ying Shi did a great deal, and he also made great contributions to the country. I have described this in detail on May 18th at the foundation stone laying ceremony. I hope that all the old friends and comrades of Mr. Ying Shi and all the people of Shanghai will not change their original intentions and will support Chiang Kai-shek with the spirit of supporting Mr. Ying Shi in those years to fulfill Mr. Ying Shi's unfulfilled wishes (to follow the Leader's teachings and realize the Three Principles of the People in China). This is the blessing of the country and the fortune of our party. Furthermore, the establishment of this memorial tower has been laborious for the Shanghai Municipal Government to sponsor, so it can be completed as scheduled. Also, today's opening ceremony has been warmly attended by comrades, and there are also those who have come from afar. I would like to express my sincere gratitude to everyone.

Pan Gongzhan's Speech: Following that, Mr. Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, briefly stating that the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters is greatly honored to attend the completion ceremony of the Ying Shi Memorial Tower today. The three gentlemen Chiang, Huang, and Zhang donated funds to build this magnificent memorial tower, and their intention is not simply to commemorate Mr. Ying Shi's past achievements. They also want to take this opportunity to encourage all the comrades who died later in our party and the revolutionary people of the whole country to rise up and emulate Mr. Ying Shi. Mr. Yingbai has already mentioned this, but there are many words and deeds in Mr. Ying Shi's life that can be used as our example. Now, I dare to put forward the two most important points as a warning to all comrades. First, Mr. Ying Shi is the most faithful person to the Leader and obeys the Leader without changing. After the failure of the second revolution in the year of Gui Chou, some comrades in our party doubted the Leader's ideology or policies, not to mention the people. However, Mr. Ying Shi firmly believed that only by believing in Sun Yat-sen's ideology and obeying his leadership can a new China be built. The long letter he wrote to Mr. Huang Keqiang clearly shows that Mr. Ying Shi's ability to struggle for the revolution to the end and achieve something lies entirely in this firm belief. Mr. Dai Jitao said that if there is no mutual trust, there will be no mutual trust. If we want to emulate Mr. Ying Shi, we should first emulate his behavior of firmly believing in ideology and obeying the leader. Second, the Leader's legacy once said that everyone should aim to serve and not to seize. Mr. Ying Shi strictly abides by the discipline of the group and engages in struggle to achieve the goal of serving the people, but he never wants to seize any benefits from the people for his own private possession. This can be proved by his life history and the situation of his family after his death. If we join this party and want to use this combined group to obtain special benefits without intending to serve the people, it is definitely not what we should emulate from Mr. Ying Shi. I hope that in the future, all those who admire this memorial tower will at least learn the two most valuable spirits of Mr. Ying Shi, then the construction of the Three Principles of the People can be successful in the end, and the construction of this memorial tower will not be in vain.

Speeches by Guests: In addition, Central Committee members Li Liejun and Li Shizeng, Legislative Committee member Jiao Yitang and other gentlemen all gave extremely sorrowful speeches, the general meaning of which was that the construction of this tower is to commemorate Mr. Chen Ying Shi's past achievements and to encourage those who died later to take responsibility for realizing the Three Principles of the People. The ceremony was completed after eleven o'clock.

Another message: President of the Judicial Yuan Wang Chonghui was unable to come to Shanghai to participate in the grand ceremony due to matters and sent a telegram to Mayor Zhang to express his apology. The original telegram is as follows: Shanghai Municipal Office, Mayor Zhang Yuejun Brother Xun Jian. Today is the completion ceremony of the Chen Gong Ying Shi Memorial Tower. Your brother was unable to go to Shanghai to participate due to matters and sent a telegram to apologize. Please forgive me. Wang Chonghui Jiang Yin.

Borrowing the Balance of Rent

Exchange for Municipal Public Bonds 162

The Municipal Government Announced Yesterday

The Municipal Government previously decided to borrow a small amount of rent to raise the short-term tariff treasury bonds for the 19th year in accordance with the order, and since September 30th, it has been borrowing and collecting for two months by the Finance Bureau and various collection offices. However, the total amount of rent in this city in two months is about one million or more, excluding the exchange of tariff treasury bonds, there is a slight balance. Now, after the Municipal Public Bond Solicitation Committee suggested exchanging it for municipal public bonds, the Municipal Construction Discussion Committee decided to pass it. The Municipal Government stated that the above-mentioned method of exchanging for municipal public bonds does not increase the burden on the citizens, and municipal construction can be expected to be realized soon. It has replied and ordered the Finance Bureau to comply with it. (The Municipal Government's announcement can be found in the advertising column)

Yesterday's Social Bureau

Convened a Meeting to Promote the National Calendar 163

Page 14

Yesterday, the Social Bureau specially convened people from all walks of life in the bureau's conference room to discuss the promotion of the National Calendar. Ma Liutang, Zhang Zhenyuan, Zhang Yaoming of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhang Junpu of the Public Security Bureau, Zheng Chengqing of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other 20 people attended. Feng Liutang chaired the meeting, and the chairman reported that the calendar is the national standard and should be earnestly observed. The chairman then asked everyone for their opinions on how to promote it among the general public. The discussion then began, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Each representative present shall submit their promotion methods to the meeting within three days; (2) The second meeting is scheduled for next Monday. The meeting adjourned at 5 p.m.

The army officials sent by the central government to Japan to observe the autumn military exercises, Qian Dajun, Chen Cheng, Yang Guanyu, and the accompanying personnel Zhao Yiguang, Zhao Yunpeng, Mao Bangchu, Liu Fangxiu, Liu Hua, Li Guoliang, and Pan Jing, etc., have come to Shanghai from Beijing and purchased first-class berths on the Shanghai Maru at the local Nippon Yusen Kaisha office. American Ambassador to Arrive in Shanghai Tomorrow 165

Promotion Expected After Approximately One Examination Period

According to the message from the American Consulate General, American Ambassador Johnson and several staff members took the Fengtian ship south from Tianjin a few days ago and will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow (the 5th). After the First Secretary of the American Embassy, ​​Shi Baike, took leave to return to the country, he happened to be passing through Shanghai on his way back to his post. At that time, he will go to the dock with the American Consul General and others to welcome the American Ambassador. It is not yet known where the American Ambassador will go after arriving in Shanghai. It is expected that he will stay for a week or ten days before going to Beijing. It is not yet known whether there are any special issues to discuss with the National Government, but according to Tianjin news, the American Ambassador is quite concerned about the safety and protection of American missionaries in areas where the bandit atmosphere has not been quelled.

National Ships to Be Developed

Weihaiwei Passenger Ship 166

Recovering Lost Shipping Rights

The port of Weihaiwei has historically had no Chinese ships operating, and shipping rights have long been in foreign hands. Due to the presence of British warships stationed at Liugong Island, and officials and trading houses based in Weihaiwei, Shanghai-based Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire both dispatched formal passenger ships on regular routes. These operated on average thirteen or fourteen times a month. Now that Weihaiwei has been taken over by our country, and the northern coast of China is without any domestic ships, there are plans to launch a shipping service. What we have heard is recorded below.

British Ships Cease Operation of Mail. Correspondence and mail between Shanghai and Weihaiwei have historically been entrusted to British trading companies such as Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire due to the lack of regularly scheduled Chinese ships operating from this port. Now that the British government has returned Weihaiwei, British merchants such as Butterfield & Swire continue to operate ships to Weihaiwei, but they have ceased carrying mail. Currently, the postal authorities are

Temporarily Entrusting Non-Regular Chinese Ships to Transport Mail. Chinese Ships Planning Shipping Routes. Weihaiwei has been taken over by our country. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, being a state-run shipping company, has now assigned the "Xinfeng" and "Xinming" ships of the Northern Shipping Fleet to operate in Weihaiwei. They plan to follow the Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson's northern China routes and add Weihaiwei as an additional port of call. The business department of the company is already planning this. As Weihaiwei lacks a branch office, they plan to set up a management office to handle cargo transport and passenger services. The first step will be to liaise with the postal authorities.

Requesting Subsidies for the China Merchants. For the sake of opening a Shanghai-

Weihaiwei route, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is planning comprehensively. As there are fewer goods and passengers at that location, they will begin by taking over the mail transport formerly handled by British ships. The business department of the company has already sent a letter to the Postal Administration, stating that they will handle the transportation of mail to Weihaiwei and requesting, in addition to transport fees, an annual subsidy of two thousand taels from the postal authorities to support business operations. This letter has been sent, and they will proceed with launching the shipping service as soon as a reply is received.

Case of Dutch Ship Insulting Ms. Xiao 167

Chief Officer Dismissed, Crew Demoted. Xiao's Relatives Form Support Association. The chief officer of the "Tjipondok" of the Java China Japan Lijn, Lan Anqi (H.W.Dyaing),

The case of insulting Ms. Xiao has aroused the resistance of the national public. Yesterday, the ship arrived in Shanghai from Java again. A reporter visited the ship's comprador, He Fenteng, who said that there was already a considerable solution to this case. What he knew is recorded below.

Chief Officer Dismissed. The principal offender in the Xiao case was the chief officer, Lan

Anqi. After protests from various Chinese public organizations and further opposition from all sectors of Xiamen, who severed economic ties with the company, the Java head office, knowing that they had offended the public, dismissed the offending chief officer, Lan Anqi, and appointed a replacement who is already in the process of taking over.

Remaining Crew Demoted. Those implicated in this case include the second officer, Lei Dimai (J.C.Rademakw), and the shipowner, Ya Ershi (D.R.Als), who also bears considerable responsibility. The doctor, Bai Lingu (G.H.bringcw), provided a false report. The head office has ordered that they all be demoted. The new shipowner, second officer, and ship doctor will take over their duties in Shanghai tomorrow.

Written Apology Sent to Shanghai. According to Mr. He, after the incident where the chief officer kissed Ms. Xiao, the head office personally apologized to Ms. Xiao to settle the matter. The Macau Chamber of Commerce also knew about this situation and sent a telegram to prove it. The written decisions of the head office regarding the punishment of the offending crew members will also be sent to Shanghai next week for publication.

Reception for Various Sectors. The Java China Japan Lijn, believing that this case has been handled properly, and to make the truth known to various sectors in Shanghai and restore good relations between China and the Netherlands, has scheduled a reception on the "Tjipondok" tomorrow, which is docked at the China Merchants Wharf. Investigation by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce

Situation of Silk Mill Workers' Unemployment 173

Shanghai silk mills have suffered a sharp decline in sales of foreign raw silk. Their funds have been depleted and they can no longer maintain operations. There is a consensus to suspend operations. After investigation by Shen Huachen, chairman and committee member of the Shanghai Silk Mill Trade Association, it was found that there are 106 silk mills in Shanghai. If all of them suspend operations, more than 100,000 male and female workers will have no way to make a living, which will have a significant impact on social order. He specially advised the larger mills, such as Ruilun, to continue operations to maintain the status quo. As the overseas silk market is becoming increasingly sluggish and there is no way to maintain support, Ruilun and other mills all suspended operations on the 31st of last month, and the situation is becoming more serious. After reporting the suspension of work by various factories, the standing committee members of the Silk Mill Trade Association, with Chairman Shen and others having gone to Beijing to petition, were unable to determine when government relief funds would be issued and the situation was fraught with danger. They telegraphed Chairman Shen Huachen at the Capital Central Hotel in the capital the day before yesterday, reporting everything. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce also paid special attention to the sudden increase of more than 100,000 unemployed workers in Shanghai due to the closure of all silk mills and sent a special commissioner to Shanghai to investigate the situation.

Obtaining Overseas Passports Through Deception 176

Strictly Crack Down to Prevent Being Deceived. Shanghai Public Security Bureau inspectors recently seized passports issued by the Singapore Consulate on a French mail ship from peddlers and merchants from Zhejiang who were going abroad to do business. The ages and circumstances did not match, and there was evidence of photo switching. The four peddlers and merchants were detained and taken to the bureau for investigation.

The clues for the crackdown originated from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's strict crackdown on passports for peddlers going abroad after the Municipal Government forwarded a strict order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. As a result, various peddlers and merchants had no way to apply for passports, but their desire to go abroad to do business was strong. Therefore, they sought help everywhere, resulting in hundreds of existing "agents" (i.e., those who arranged passports) trying to find ways. Later, they learned that it was easier to apply for passports from the issuing authorities in Guangdong Province, so they flocked to Guangdong to apply. The Guangdong Municipal Government, suspecting that the merchants were from Zhejiang and should apply for passports in Shanghai instead of traveling to Guangdong, inquired with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs about the truth and suspended issuing passports. However, the "agents" found out that the consulates in Nanyang islands, such as Singapore and Penang, were even more lenient in issuing passports. They purchased many photos of others with upright features and western clothing and went to the consulates in those places to apply, costing only seven yuan per passport (because this type of passport was not issued by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs but was a temporarily printed sheet of paper). After obtaining the passports, they returned to Shanghai and sold them, requiring only that the age be similar. They tore off the original photos, pasted on photos of the passport buyers, and added a forged round seal, making it difficult to detect even with careful examination. Many people have been able to go abroad through deception. This time, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau acted on a tip-off and went to investigate, successfully cracking down on the scheme.

Thoroughly Investigate the Comprador and Those Hiding Gold Bars. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau has recently received anonymous letters reporting that it has conducted several investigations, but there have been no clues. Furthermore, the peddlers and merchants who were willing to go abroad to do business have remained silent. After taking one of the arrested persons to the bureau and handing him over to the Third Section for interrogation, he confessed the hidden details and revealed who he had bought the passport from, a man surnamed Gao. Detectives were dispatched to arrest him, but he had already fled.

The "Agents" in Shanghai Have All Fled. Since this case occurred, the "agents" fled in fear of being implicated after hearing of Gao's arrest. The peddlers from Zhejiang who came to Shanghai to apply for passports and go abroad usually lived in the houses or exchange shops established by the "agents" (because the peddlers remitted the money they earned abroad to the "agents," who then remitted it back home. They never stayed in other hotels or inns, so they had good access to information). It is now reported that the Shanghai Public Security Bureau is still detaining the four peddlers and merchants and interrogating them closely, intending to thoroughly investigate and eliminate evil.

The Value of Passports and Tickets. Before the crackdown, it cost peddlers at most 220-230 yuan to entrust an "agent" to apply for a passport and purchase a ticket. Now, due to the strictness, the price has risen to 300-400 yuan for applying in other ports, yet people are still scrambling to do so.

Why Not Take a Ship from the Place Where the Passport is Issued? Because buying a ticket in ports such as Hong Kong, Singapore, and Penang requires buying a third-class ticket, while buying a through ticket in Shanghai is cheaper than a third-class ticket by 30-40%. It is even cheaper to smuggle gold bars without a passport, but those with sufficient money are unwilling to take the risk.

What Will Happen Next? It is reported that the Shanghai Public Security Bureau is now strictly cracking down on this kind of matter, striving to eliminate it completely so as to prevent ignorant villagers from being deceived and to ensure public safety.

Local News

Heartbreaking Sight: Twenty-One Corpses 180

Mortality Reached Thirty Percent

Cries Fill the Scene at the Morgue

Insufficient Prevention Beforehand

Authorities Should Seek Proper Handling Afterward

On the chillingly windy Republican Road yesterday, twenty-one corpses were laid out, their charred and disfigured state juxtaposed with the ashes and debris of the burned military uniforms, a heartbreaking sight that filled one with sorrow. Of these twenty-one corpses, fifteen have been identified. Excluding three children aged three and one, the rest were women who made a living through their own labor. Having been burned by the fire, their eyes and ears were indistinguishable, their bodies like charred charcoal. Cries filled the scene at the identification site, echoing each other. Onlookers could not help but feel a pang of grief. The day before yesterday, when the fire broke out, these female workers cried out to escape. Yesterday, the living mourned the corpses. During these twenty-four hours, the sounds of lamentation and weeping near the Fuchang Military Clothing Factory seemed to have been uninterrupted. The factory had a total of over a hundred female workers. About seven died in the hospital in the past two days. Adding the twenty-one corpses found at the fire site yesterday, the number of deaths due to the disaster has reached around twenty-eight. The number of remaining unknown deaths is not included. Therefore, the number of deaths in this incident accounts for at least 30% of the total number of workers, which is truly shocking.

Searching for Corpses in the Rubble. After the fire at the Third Fuchang Military Clothing Factory, the residents of Zhabei, because of the unusual disaster, all had a desire to witness the aftermath to widen their horizons. Therefore, yesterday, from morning to dusk, the number of onlookers on Republican Road was endless. The Fourth District Public Security Bureau specially hired twelve workers to sift through the rubble for corpses. From morning until dusk, a total of twenty-one corpses were found, mostly with incomplete clothing, withered hair, and terrifying faces. The timid dared not approach. When excavating the ashes, bricks, and tiles, there were police officers and members of the security corps directing and supervising. However, the families of the victims had already arrived at the fire site crying, eager to identify the bodies. Therefore, as soon as a corpse was found, the relatives gathered around. Husbands cried for their wives, and children cried for their mothers. Of the twenty-one corpses, except for three or four child corpses, the rest were mostly pitiful women.

Thirty Percent Died in the Fire. Workers moved the corpses one by one, placing them by the roadside for families to identify them. They were separated with lead sheets for identification and arranged in the order they were found. The names of the fifteen identified corpses are as follows: Wang Da Caizi, 18 years old, female, from Yancheng; Wang Yuan Shi, 44 years old, from Taizhou; Zhao Xiao Dangzi, 17 years old, female, from Yancheng; Jiang Liudi, 13 years old, female, from Tongzhou; Wang Cuilian, 12 years old, female; Peng Xiaoyang, 12 years old, female, from Yancheng; Guo Tian Shi, 42 years old, from Tongzhou; Guo Shoeszi, 5 years old; Wang Sun Shi, 26 years old, from Yancheng; Wang Hongzi, 5 years old; Wang Koufuchang, the tragic scene of the military uniform factory being destroyed (taken by Zhonghua); the tragic scene of the military uniform factory being destroyed (taken by Zhonghua); Z, 3 years old; Liu Sun Shi, 27 years old, from Yancheng; Guo Zhu Shi, 23 years old, from Yancheng; Chen Gengcheng, 3 years old; Mao Wang Shi, 23 years old, from Funing. The deceased in the hospital: One from the Red Cross Hospital, Lu Gao Shi. In addition to the two from the day before yesterday, the Pushan Hospital had Yuan Zhu Shi, 46 years old, from Yong, and Yuan Xiao Nu, 5 years old. Baolong Hospital: Chen Xia Shi and Wang Cailin. Currently, the known number of deaths is nearly thirty, which accounts for almost 30% of all the female workers in the factory. Over sixty were burned by the fire. Yesterday, there were still many people going to Pushan Hospital for follow-up examinations. An entire mother and daughter were burned to death. Most of those burned were women and children. Guo Tian Shi and Guo Shoeszi, mentioned above, are mother and daughter. Tian Shi was working and brought her daughter to the factory to play. Even more tragic was the case of Wang Sun Shi, Wang Hongzi, and Wang Kouzi, a mother and her two daughters, who all died in the fire at the same time. Wang Sun Shi's husband, Wang Shanting, a leather worker, lived at No. 3, Lane 2219, Meiyuan Road. Hongzi was five years old and Kouzi was three years old. Of the four members of the family, three have already died, which is no less than the collapse of the entire family in one fire. Mao Wang Shi, Wang Sun Shi, Kouzi, Hongzi, Liu Sun Shi, and Guo Tian Shi of the twenty-one corpses were reported by the 27th Bao, 11th Yuan Dibao to the court, which dispatched Prosecutor Yang accompanied by Examiner Shen to the scene to verify the cause of death and allow the families to collect the bodies separately. The remaining corpses will be verified later.

Lack of Preparedness Caused This Disaster. The magnitude of the disaster caused by this fire is truly rare in recent years. The losses of the Fuchang Military Clothing Factory, such as cotton, military uniforms, and buildings, are worth tens of thousands of yuan, but they are limited. However, the loss of life on the workers' side accounts for 30% of the total number of workers, and the fact that all the dead are women and children is even more tragic. The factory uses cotton to remake military uniforms, and the amount of cotton and clothing materials stored on weekdays is very large. The lack of fire-fighting equipment inevitably led to this disaster. The panic and confusion of the female workers upon seeing the fire was also expected. If more Taiping gates could be opened and there was more emergency training in peacetime, there might not have been so many deaths. It is said that the factory only has one back door staircase, which is very narrow, and a large amount of cotton and military uniforms are piled up. Even in normal times, there is hardly any space to turn around. It is easy to imagine the situation of being crowded and unable to move in a rush. Some workers who escaped said that the cause of the fire was a cigarette. However, after the fire broke out, the factory managers not only did not order the female workers to escape but temporarily closed the doors, as if afraid that the goods would be lost, leading to an uncontrollable situation. If this statement is accurate, then the dead are even more pitiful. There must be many similar factories in the city that are not properly equipped. It is hoped that the authorities can properly plan safety measures and ensure the safety of the workers.
